==> Caveats
Python is installed as
  /opt/homebrew/bin/python3.11

Unversioned and major-versioned symlinks `python`, `python3`, `python-config`, `python3-config`, `pip`, `pip3`, etc. pointing to
`python3.11`, `python3.11-config`, `pip3.11` etc., respectively, are installed into
  /opt/homebrew/opt/python@3.11/libexec/bin

You can install Python packages with
  pip3.11 install <package>
They will install into the site-package directory
  /opt/homebrew/lib/python3.11/site-packages

`idle3.11` requires tkinter, which is available separately:
  brew install python-tk@3.11

gdbm (`dbm.gnu`) is no longer included in this formula, but it is available separately:
  brew install python-gdbm@3.11
`dbm.ndbm` changed database backends in Homebrew Python 3.11.
If you need to read a database from a previous Homebrew Python created via `dbm.ndbm`,
you'll need to read your database using the older version of Homebrew Python and convert to another format.
`dbm` still defaults to `dbm.gnu` when it is installed.

If you do not need a specific version of Python, and always want Homebrew's `python3` in your PATH:
  brew install python3

For more information about Homebrew and Python, see: https://docs.brew.sh/Homebrew-and-Python

naomirusch@localhost paperscout % poetry run python - <<'PY'
from paperscout.sources.crossref import fetch_from_crossref
from paperscout.exporters.excel import export_excel
from paperscout.pipeline import dedup_by_doi
import pandas as pd

since = "2025-09-01"
rows = 50
journals = pd.read_excel("journals_from_upload.xlsx")["Journal"].dropna().unique().tolist()

all_articles = []
for j in journals:
    try:
        print(f"Ziehe: {j}")
        all_articles += fetch_from_crossref(journal=j, rows=rows, since=since)
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Fehler bei {j}: {e}")

deduped = dedup_by_doi(all_articles)
export_excel(deduped, "results.xlsx")
print("Fertig: results.xlsx")
PY

    args = p.parse_args()

    journals = pd.read_excel(args.journals_file)["Journal"].dropna().unique().tolist()
    all_articles = []
    for j in journals:
        print(f"Ziehe: {j}")
        try:
            all_articles += fetch_from_crossref(journal=j, rows=args.rows, since=args.since)
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Fehler bei {j}: {e}")

    export_excel(dedup_by_doi(all_articles), args.out)
    print(f"Fertig: {args.out}")

from paperscout.sources.crossref_strict import fetch_from_crossref_strict
from paperscout.exporters.excel import export_excel
from paperscout.pipeline import dedup_by_doi
import pandas as pd

since = "2025-09-01"
rows = 150
journals = pd.read_excel("~/Downloads/Journal Service _Oktober.xlsx")["Journal"].dropna().unique().tolist()

all_articles = []
for j in journals:
    try:
        print(f"Ziehe: {j}")
        all_articles += fetch_from_crossref_strict(journal=j, rows=rows, since=since)
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Fehler bei {j}: {e}")

export_excel(dedup_by_doi(all_articles), "results_strict.xlsx")
print("âœ… Fertig: results_strict.xlsx")

from paperscout.sources.crossref_strict import fetch_from_crossref_strict
from paperscout.exporters.excel import export_excel
from paperscout.pipeline import dedup_by_doi
import pandas as pd

since = "2025-09-01"
rows = 150
journals = pd.read_excel("journals_input.xlsx")["Journal"].dropna().unique().tolist()

all_articles = []
for j in journals:
    try:
        print(f"Ziehe: {j}")
        all_articles += fetch_from_crossref_strict(journal=j, rows=rows, since=since)
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Fehler bei {j}: {e}")

export_excel(dedup_by_doi(all_articles), "results_strict.xlsx")
print("âœ… Fertig: results_strict.xlsx")
